## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy xDS v3 Transport Protocol Implementation

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement the xDS v3 transport protocol. Identify: the GrpcSubscriptionImpl adapter, the SotW (State of the World) GrpcMuxImpl, the Delta xDS NewGrpcMuxImpl, the GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory that selects between SotW and Delta modes, and the unified XdsMux template that supports both variants.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

## Summary of xDS v3 Transport Protocol Components

I identified **19 C++ source files** and **14 key symbols** implementing the xDS v3 transport protocol:

### **Legacy Components** (original dual-mux architecture):
1. **GrpcSubscriptionImpl** - Adapter class bridging individual subsystems to the mux
2. **GrpcMuxImpl** (legacy) - State-of-the-World (SotW) gRPC mux
3. **NewGrpcMuxImpl** - Delta xDS mux implementation
4. **GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory** - Factory selecting between SotW and Delta modes

### **Unified Template Components** (migration architecture):
5. **GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS>** - Generic template parameterized by subscription state, factory, request, and response types
6. **GrpcMuxSotw** - Template specialization for SotW protocol
7. **GrpcMuxDelta** - Template specialization for Delta protocol
8. **BaseSubscriptionState<RS,RQ>** - Abstract base for protocol state machines
9. **SotwSubscriptionState** - SotW-specific state machine
10. **DeltaSubscriptionState** - Delta-specific state machine (XdsMux version)

### **Key Files Located**:
- Core implementations in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`
- Unified templates in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/`
- Supporting infrastructure: WatchMap, factories, and state management

The implementation shows Envoy's migration from a dual-mux system to a unified template-based design, controlled by the `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux` runtime flag.

Envoy is organized across two distinct architectures: a legacy dual-mux system and a unified template-based system.\\n\\nLEGACY COMPONENTS:\\n\\n1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc): The adapter class that wraps either a legacy GrpcMuxImpl or NewGrpcMuxImpl. It implements the Subscription interface and provides the bridge between individual subsystems (LDS, CDS, EDS, etc.) and the underlying mux implementation.\\n\\n2. GrpcMuxImpl - SotW (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy State-of-the-World (SotW) gRPC mux implementation. It manages subscriptions to resources over a single gRPC stream using the DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse protocol. It maintains transport-level concerns like stream management, queueing logic, and multiplexing.\\n\\n3. NewGrpcMuxImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy Delta xDS mux implementation. It handles incremental xDS updates using DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse messages, managing resource additions and removals more efficiently than SotW.\\n\\n4. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): The legacy delta protocol state machine that tracks subscription state for the NewGrpcMuxImpl.\\n\\n5. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory and DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc): Factories that instantiate either GrpcMuxImpl (SotW) or NewGrpcMuxImpl (Delta) based on configuration or runtime flags, providing the selection logic between the two modes.\\n\\nUNIFIED TEMPLATE-BASED COMPONENTS:\\n\\n6. GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The unified generic template that abstracts over subscription state type (S), state factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). This replaces the need for separate legacy implementations.\\n\\n7. GrpcMuxSotw (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for SotW: GrpcMuxImpl<SotwSubscriptionState, SotwSubscriptionStateFactory, DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified SotW implementation.\\n\\n8. GrpcMuxDelta (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for Delta: GrpcMuxImpl<DeltaSubscriptionState, DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified Delta implementation.\\n\\n9. BaseSubscriptionState<RS,RQ> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract base class for protocol state machines, parameterized by response type (RS) and request type (RQ). It handles protocol-agnostic concerns like nonce tracking, error handling, and TTL management.\\n\\n10. SubscriptionStateFactory<T> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract factory template for creating SubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n11. SotwSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DiscoveryResponse, DiscoveryRequest>. Implements the SotW protocol state machine with full state tracking and update generation logic.\\n\\n12. SotwSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for SotwSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n13. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DeltaDiscoveryResponse, DeltaDiscoveryRequest>. Implements the Delta protocol state machine with resource set tracking (added/removed/removed_resources).\\n\\n14. DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for DeltaSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n\\n15. WatchMap (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc): Manages subscriptions from multiple clients (watches) for a given resource type and dispatches updates to each.\\n\\nARCHITECTURE NOTES:\\n\\nThe codebase is currently in a migration phase from the legacy dual-mux system (GrpcMuxImpl and NewGrpcMuxImpl) to the unified template-based system (GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta). The factory in grpc_subscription_factory.cc selects between implementations based on the envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux runtime flag. Both systems coexist to enable gradual migration.\\n\\nThe template design allows both SotW and Delta variants to share transport-level logic (gRPC stream management, queuing, watch management) while specializing for protocol-specific state management. Each SubscriptionState type encapsulates the protocol-specific logic for handling discovery responses, managing subscription interest, and generating requests.\"\n}\n",

GrpcMuxDelta (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for Delta: GrpcMuxImpl<DeltaSubscriptionState, DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse>. WatchMap (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc): Manages subscriptions from multiple clients (watches) for a given resource type and dispatches updates to each.\\n\\nARCHITECTURE NOTES:\\n\\nThe codebase is currently in a migration phase from the legacy dual-mux system (GrpcMuxImpl and NewGrpcMuxImpl) to the unified template-based system (GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta). The factory in grpc_subscription_factory.cc selects between implementations based on the envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux runtime flag. Both systems coexist to enable gradual migration.\\n\\nThe template design allows both SotW and Delta variants to share transport-level logic (gRPC stream management, queuing, watch management) while specializing for protocol-specific state management. Each SubscriptionState type encapsulates the protocol-specific logic for handling discovery responses, managing subscription interest, and generating requests.\"\n}\n",
